# SWING_LOOKBACK_4H_BARS sweep — may4_full_bars.csv replay

Walk-forward BOS simulation. Cooldown: 4h per direction. Min history before first eval: 80h. Only the 4h lookback knob varies — 1h path uses defaults (lookback=24, validation=2, range=1.2×).

**Reading guide**: Under current (4h-priority) code, a shorter 4h lookback doesn't add many *new* alerts — it mostly re-tags events from `1h` to `4h` (more structural conviction, tighter level for the trade plan). The 'Net new fires' column below isolates the genuine pickup.

## Summary

| Lookback | Days | Total fires | 4h-tagged | 1h-tagged | Net new vs LB=30 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 15 | 2.5d | 3443 | 1446 | 1997 | +62 |
| 20 | 3.3d | 3430 | 1227 | 2203 | +48 |
| 25 | 4.2d | 3411 | 1016 | 2395 | +25 |
| 30 | 5.0d | 3388 | 848 | 2540 | +0 |
